Uncmpindex.java
Includes code to compress the tokens in Cranfield documents using Block Compression and Front Coding algorithm.The documents are converted to lemmas and stems 
and indexed accordingly. The words are hyphens are treated as a single word (Example: kick-start is treated as kickstart).
The words from stopwords file and common_words file taken from /people/cs/s/sanda/cs6322/resourcesIR are removed from tokens list.

Porter.java
Implementation of Porters Stemming algorithm to obtain the root of a given word.

The readme file has the command for compiling and running the java code
